 i=mcfr401 o=mcfrout401 runtpe=mcfrtpe401 tasks 8

         1-       -*-mcnpgen-*- 2000MWth MCFR with LME 60cm 14m3 w/ control,n+p                   
         2-       c mcnp6 i=mcfr270.txt o=mcfrout270.txt runtpe=mcfrtpe270.txt                    
         3-       c                                                                               
         4-       c Notes about input file:                                                       
         5-       c                                                                               
         6-       c The control rods are positioned fully withdrawn at T=850 C.                   
         7-       c Begin burn-up with reprocessing 2nd iteration (Day 100)                       
         8-       c                                                                               
         9-       c Boron carbide was added 60 cm above the bottom of the TZM end.                
        10-       c                                                                               
        11-       c The control blades in the reflector region were removedper Nick Smith's       
        12-       c remarks of having a second system that may be unnessary and prone to issues.  
        13-       c                                                                               
        14-       c This input file evaluates a 14m^3 volume core with a fuel mixture of          
        15-       c 45.2 NaCl - 46 UCl3 - 8.65(TRU)Cl3. The TRU composition used was              
        16-       c provided in the REBUS-3700 design concept. The above fuel composition         
        17-       c was chosen to increase the amount of U-238 in the fuel and keep the           
        18-       c melting point below 650 C.                                                    
        19-       c                                                                               
        20-       c The geometry of the core is simply a cylinder core with a TZM vessel and      
        21-       c a 60 cm thick lead-magnesium eutectic (LME) reflector outside of the core.    
        22-       c A B4C poison was added beyond the reflector to act a shield and also reduce   
        23-       c the chance of criticality in the heat exchanger.                              
        24-       c                                                                               
        25-       c There are four outlet pipes and four inlet pipes into the core filled with    
        26-       c fuel salts. There are control blades of various compositions located in the   
        27-       c reflector region.                                                             
        28-       c                                                                               
        29-       c                                                                               
        30-       c ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        31-       c Cells                                                                         
        32-       c ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        33-       c                                                                               
        34-       c ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        35-       c In Core Fuel Salts                                                            
        36-       c ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        37-       c The 100 series of cells are in the fuel salts in the core. In                 
        38-       c the core there are a total of 50 cells of varying densities and temperatures  
        39-       c because the fuel density is highly temperature dependant. This allows for an  
        40-       c improved power density model of the core. Making this mesh there are 10 axial 
        41-       c nodes and 5 radial nodes.                                                     
        42-       c                                                                               
        43-       c In the in-core region (directly below) the cells are broken into the five radi
        44-       c nodes in each axial node. Thus Node 1 is the bottom axial node and cell 100 is
        45-       c center cell of the fuel first axial node (bottom center of core).             
        46-       c                                                                               
        47-       c --------------------------                                                    
        48-       c Bottom Fuel Regions: Node 1                                                   
        49-       c --------------------------
